71
72static inline int
73arena_avail_comp(arena_chunk_map_t *a, arena_chunk_map_t *b)
74{
75 int ret;
76 size_t a_size = a->bits & ~PAGE_MASK((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1));
77 size_t b_size = b->bits & ~PAGE_MASK((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1));
78
79 ret = (a_size > b_size) - (a_size < b_size);
80 if (ret == 0) {
81 uintptr_t a_mapelm, b_mapelm;
82
83 if ((a->bits & CHUNK_MAP_KEY((size_t)0x1U)) != CHUNK_MAP_KEY((size_t)0x1U))
84 a_mapelm = (uintptr_t)a;
85 else {
86 /*
87 * Treat keys as though they are lower than anything
88 * else.
89 */
90 a_mapelm = 0;
91 }
92 b_mapelm = (uintptr_t)b;
93
94 ret = (a_mapelm > b_mapelm) - (a_mapelm < b_mapelm);
95 }
96
97 return (ret);
98}

103
104static inline int
105arena_chunk_dirty_comp(arena_chunk_t *a, arena_chunk_t *b)
106{
107
108 assert(a != NULL)do { if (config_debug && !(a != ((void*)0))) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 108, "a != NULL"); abort(); } } while (0);
109 assert(b != NULL)do { if (config_debug && !(b != ((void*)0))) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 109, "b != NULL"); abort(); } } while (0);
110
111 /*
112 * Short-circuit for self comparison. The following comparison code
113 * would come to the same result, but at the cost of executing the slow
114 * path.
115 */
116 if (a == b)
117 return (0);
118
119 /*
120 * Order such that chunks with higher fragmentation are "less than"
121 * those with lower fragmentation -- purging order is from "least" to
122 * "greatest". Fragmentation is measured as:
123 *
124 * mean current avail run size
125 * --------------------------------
126 * mean defragmented avail run size
127 *
128 * navail
129 * -----------
130 * nruns_avail nruns_avail-nruns_adjac
131 * = ========================= = -----------------------
132 * navail nruns_avail
133 * -----------------------
134 * nruns_avail-nruns_adjac
135 *
136 * The following code multiplies away the denominator prior to
137 * comparison, in order to avoid division.
138 *
139 */
140 {
141 size_t a_val = (a->nruns_avail - a->nruns_adjac) *
142 b->nruns_avail;
143 size_t b_val = (b->nruns_avail - b->nruns_adjac) *
144 a->nruns_avail;
145
146 if (a_val < b_val)
147 return (1);
148 if (a_val > b_val)
149 return (-1);
150 }
151 /*
152 * Break ties by chunk address. For fragmented chunks, report lower
153 * addresses as "lower", so that fragmentation reduction happens first
154 * at lower addresses. However, use the opposite ordering for
155 * unfragmented chunks, in order to increase the chances of
156 * re-allocating dirty runs.
157 */
158 {
159 uintptr_t a_chunk = (uintptr_t)a;
160 uintptr_t b_chunk = (uintptr_t)b;
161 int ret = ((a_chunk > b_chunk) - (a_chunk < b_chunk));
162 if (a->nruns_adjac == 0) {
163 assert(b->nruns_adjac == 0)do { if (config_debug && !(b->nruns_adjac == 0)) {
je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 163, "b->nruns_adjac == 0"); abort(); } }
while (0);
164 ret = -ret;
165 }
166 return (ret);
167 }
168}

174static inline bool_Bool
175arena_avail_adjac_pred(arena_chunk_t *chunk, size_t pageind)
176{
177 bool_Bool ret;
178
179 if (pageind-1 < map_biasje_map_bias)
180 ret = false0;
181 else {
182 ret = (arena_mapbits_allocated_getje_arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk, pageind-1) == 0);
183 assert(ret == false || arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk,do { if (config_debug && !(ret == 0 || je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, pageind-1) != je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind
))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 184, "ret == false || arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind-1) != arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
184 pageind-1) != arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind))do { if (config_debug && !(ret == 0 || je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, pageind-1) != je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind
))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 184, "ret == false || arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind-1) != arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
185 }
186 return (ret);
187}

200 != arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind+npages))do { if (config_debug && !(ret == 0 || je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get

201 }

205static inline bool_Bool
206arena_avail_adjac(arena_chunk_t *chunk, size_t pageind, size_t npages)
207{
208
209 return (arena_avail_adjac_pred(chunk, pageind) ||
210 arena_avail_adjac_succ(chunk, pageind, npages));
211}
212
213static void
214arena_avail_insert(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, size_t pageind,
215 size_t npages, bool_Bool maybe_adjac_pred, bool_Bool maybe_adjac_succ)
216{
217
218 assert(npages == (arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, pageind) >>do { if (config_debug && !(npages == (je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, pageind) >> 12))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 219, "npages == (arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, pageind) >> LG_PAGE)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
219 LG_PAGE))do { if (config_debug && !(npages == (je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, pageind) >> 12))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 219, "npages == (arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, pageind) >> LG_PAGE)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
220
221 /*
222 * chunks_dirty is keyed by nruns_{avail,adjac}, so the chunk must be
223 * removed and reinserted even if the run to be inserted is clean.
224 */
225 if (chunk->ndirty != 0)
226 arena_chunk_dirty_remove(&arena->chunks_dirty, chunk);
227
228 if (maybe_adjac_pred && arena_avail_adjac_pred(chunk, pageind))
229 chunk->nruns_adjac++;
230 if (maybe_adjac_succ && arena_avail_adjac_succ(chunk, pageind, npages))
231 chunk->nruns_adjac++;
232 chunk->nruns_avail++;
233 assert(chunk->nruns_avail > chunk->nruns_adjac)do { if (config_debug && !(chunk->nruns_avail >
chunk->nruns_adjac)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 233, "chunk->nruns_avail > chunk->nruns_adjac"
); abort(); } } while (0);
234
235 if (arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind) != 0) {
236 arena->ndirty += npages;
237 chunk->ndirty += npages;
238 }
239 if (chunk->ndirty != 0)
240 arena_chunk_dirty_insert(&arena->chunks_dirty, chunk);
241
242 arena_avail_tree_insert(&arena->runs_avail, arena_mapp_getje_arena_mapp_get(chunk,
243 pageind));
244}

249{
250
251 assert(npages == (arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, pageind) >>do { if (config_debug && !(npages == (je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, pageind) >> 12))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 252, "npages == (arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, pageind) >> LG_PAGE)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
252 LG_PAGE))do { if (config_debug && !(npages == (je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, pageind) >> 12))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 252, "npages == (arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, pageind) >> LG_PAGE)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
253
254 /*
255 * chunks_dirty is keyed by nruns_{avail,adjac}, so the chunk must be
256 * removed and reinserted even if the run to be removed is clean.
257 */
258 if (chunk->ndirty != 0)
259 arena_chunk_dirty_remove(&arena->chunks_dirty, chunk);
260
261 if (maybe_adjac_pred && arena_avail_adjac_pred(chunk, pageind))
262 chunk->nruns_adjac--;
263 if (maybe_adjac_succ && arena_avail_adjac_succ(chunk, pageind, npages))
264 chunk->nruns_adjac--;
265 chunk->nruns_avail--;
266 assert(chunk->nruns_avail > chunk->nruns_adjac || (chunk->nruns_availdo { if (config_debug && !(chunk->nruns_avail >
chunk->nruns_adjac || (chunk->nruns_avail == 0 &&
chunk->nruns_adjac == 0))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 267, "chunk->nruns_avail > chunk->nruns_adjac || (chunk->nruns_avail == 0 && chunk->nruns_adjac == 0)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
267 == 0 && chunk->nruns_adjac == 0))do { if (config_debug && !(chunk->nruns_avail >
chunk->nruns_adjac || (chunk->nruns_avail == 0 &&
chunk->nruns_adjac == 0))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 267, "chunk->nruns_avail > chunk->nruns_adjac || (chunk->nruns_avail == 0 && chunk->nruns_adjac == 0)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
268
269 if (arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind) != 0) {
270 arena->ndirty -= npages;
271 chunk->ndirty -= npages;
272 }
273 if (chunk->ndirty != 0)
274 arena_chunk_dirty_insert(&arena->chunks_dirty, chunk);
275
276 arena_avail_tree_remove(&arena->runs_avail, arena_mapp_getje_arena_mapp_get(chunk,
277 pageind));
278}

280static inline void *
281arena_run_reg_alloc(arena_run_t *run, arena_bin_info_t *bin_info)
282{
283 void *ret;
284 unsigned regind;
285 bitmap_t *bitmap = (bitmap_t *)((uintptr_t)run +
286 (uintptr_t)bin_info->bitmap_offset);
287
288 assert(run->nfree > 0)do { if (config_debug && !(run->nfree > 0)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 288, "run->nfree > 0"); abort(); } } while (0);
289 assert(bitmap_full(bitmap, &bin_info->bitmap_info) == false)do { if (config_debug && !(je_bitmap_full(bitmap, &
bin_info->bitmap_info) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 289, "bitmap_full(bitmap, &bin_info->bitmap_info) == false"
); abort(); } } while (0);
290
291 regind = bitmap_sfuje_bitmap_sfu(bitmap, &bin_info->bitmap_info);
292 ret = (void *)((uintptr_t)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset +
293 (uintptr_t)(bin_info->reg_interval * regind));
294 run->nfree--;
295 if (regind == run->nextind)
296 run->nextind++;
297 assert(regind < run->nextind)do { if (config_debug && !(regind < run->nextind
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 297, "regind < run->nextind"); abort()
; } } while (0);
298 return (ret);
299}

301static inline void
302arena_run_reg_dalloc(arena_run_t *run, void *ptr)
303{
304 arena_chunk_t *chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(run)((void *)((uintptr_t)(run) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
305 size_t pageind = ((uintptr_t)ptr - (uintptr_t)chunk) >> LG_PAGE12;
306 size_t mapbits = arena_mapbits_getje_arena_mapbits_get(chunk, pageind);
307 size_t binind = arena_ptr_small_binind_getje_arena_ptr_small_binind_get(ptr, mapbits);
308 arena_bin_info_t *bin_info = &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind];
309 unsigned regind = arena_run_regindje_arena_run_regind(run, bin_info, ptr);
310 bitmap_t *bitmap = (bitmap_t *)((uintptr_t)run +
311 (uintptr_t)bin_info->bitmap_offset);
312
313 assert(run->nfree < bin_info->nregs)do { if (config_debug && !(run->nfree < bin_info
->nregs)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 313, "run->nfree < bin_info->nregs"
); abort(); } } while (0);
314 /* Freeing an interior pointer can cause assertion failure. */
315 assert(((uintptr_t)ptr - ((uintptr_t)run +do { if (config_debug && !(((uintptr_t)ptr - ((uintptr_t
)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) % (uintptr_t)bin_info
->reg_interval == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 317, "((uintptr_t)ptr - ((uintptr_t)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) % (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg_interval == 0"
); abort(); } } while (0)
316 (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) %do { if (config_debug && !(((uintptr_t)ptr - ((uintptr_t
)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) % (uintptr_t)bin_info
->reg_interval == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 317, "((uintptr_t)ptr - ((uintptr_t)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) % (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg_interval == 0"
); abort(); } } while (0)
317 (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg_interval == 0)do { if (config_debug && !(((uintptr_t)ptr - ((uintptr_t
)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) % (uintptr_t)bin_info
->reg_interval == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 317, "((uintptr_t)ptr - ((uintptr_t)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) % (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg_interval == 0"
); abort(); } } while (0);
318 assert((uintptr_t)ptr >= (uintptr_t)run +do { if (config_debug && !((uintptr_t)ptr >= (uintptr_t
)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) { je_malloc_printf

319 (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)do { if (config_debug && !((uintptr_t)ptr >= (uintptr_t
)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset)) { je_malloc_printf

, 319, "(uintptr_t)ptr >= (uintptr_t)run + (uintptr_t)bin_info->reg0_offset"
); abort(); } } while (0);

bin_info->bitmap_info, regind))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"

324 run->nfree++;
325}

327static inline void
328arena_run_zero(arena_chunk_t *chunk, size_t run_ind, size_t npages)
329{
330
331 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_UNDEFINED((void *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (run_ind <<do {} while (0)
332 LG_PAGE)), (npages << LG_PAGE))do {} while (0);
333 memset((void *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (run_ind << LG_PAGE12)), 0,
334 (npages << LG_PAGE12));
335}

339{

341 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_DEFINED((void *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (run_ind <<do {} while (0)
342 LG_PAGE)), PAGE)do {} while (0);
343}

345static inline void
346arena_run_page_validate_zeroed(arena_chunk_t *chunk, size_t run_ind)
347{
348 size_t i;
349 UNUSED__attribute__((unused)) size_t *p = (size_t *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (run_ind << LG_PAGE12));
350
351 arena_run_page_mark_zeroed(chunk, run_ind);
352 for (i = 0; i < PAGE((size_t)(1U << 12)) / sizeof(size_t); i++)
353 assert(p[i] == 0)do { if (config_debug && !(p[i] == 0)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 353, "p[i] == 0"); abort(); } } while (0);
354}

356static void
357arena_cactive_update(arena_t *arena, size_t add_pages, size_t sub_pages)
358{
359
360 if (config_stats) {
361 ssize_t cactive_diff = CHUNK_CEILING((arena->nactive +((((arena->nactive + add_pages) << 12) + je_chunksize_mask
) & ~je_chunksize_mask)
362 add_pages) << LG_PAGE)((((arena->nactive + add_pages) << 12) + je_chunksize_mask
) & ~je_chunksize_mask) - CHUNK_CEILING((arena->nactive -((((arena->nactive - sub_pages) << 12) + je_chunksize_mask
) & ~je_chunksize_mask)
363 sub_pages) << LG_PAGE)((((arena->nactive - sub_pages) << 12) + je_chunksize_mask
) & ~je_chunksize_mask);
364 if (cactive_diff != 0)
365 stats_cactive_addje_stats_cactive_add(cactive_diff);
366 }

369static void
370arena_run_split_remove(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, size_t run_ind,
371 size_t flag_dirty, size_t need_pages)
372{
373 size_t total_pages, rem_pages;
374
375 total_pages = arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_getje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind) >>
376 LG_PAGE12;
377 assert(arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+total_pages-1) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind+total_pages-1) == flag_dirty)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 378, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+total_pages-1) == flag_dirty"
); abort(); } } while (0)
378 flag_dirty)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind+total_pages-1) == flag_dirty)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 378, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+total_pages-1) == flag_dirty"
); abort(); } } while (0);
379 assert(need_pages <= total_pages)do { if (config_debug && !(need_pages <= total_pages
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 379, "need_pages <= total_pages"); abort(
); } } while (0);
380 rem_pages = total_pages - need_pages;
381
382 arena_avail_remove(arena, chunk, run_ind, total_pages, true1, true1);
383 arena_cactive_update(arena, need_pages, 0);
384 arena->nactive += need_pages;
385
386 /* Keep track of trailing unused pages for later use. */
387 if (rem_pages > 0) {
388 if (flag_dirty != 0) {
389 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk,
390 run_ind+need_pages, (rem_pages << LG_PAGE12),
391 flag_dirty);
392 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk,
393 run_ind+total_pages-1, (rem_pages << LG_PAGE12),
394 flag_dirty);
395 } else {
396 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk, run_ind+need_pages,
397 (rem_pages << LG_PAGE12),
398 arena_mapbits_unzeroed_getje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk,
399 run_ind+need_pages));
400 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk,
401 run_ind+total_pages-1, (rem_pages << LG_PAGE12),
402 arena_mapbits_unzeroed_getje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk,
403 run_ind+total_pages-1));
404 }
405 arena_avail_insert(arena, chunk, run_ind+need_pages, rem_pages,
406 false0, true1);
407 }
408}

410static void
411arena_run_split_large_helper(arena_t *arena, arena_run_t *run, size_t size,
412 bool_Bool remove, bool_Bool zero)
413{
414 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
415 size_t flag_dirty, run_ind, need_pages, i;
416
417 chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(run)((void *)((uintptr_t)(run) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
418 run_ind = (unsigned)(((uintptr_t)run - (uintptr_t)chunk) >> LG_PAGE12);
419 flag_dirty = arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind);
420 need_pages = (size >> LG_PAGE12);
421 assert(need_pages > 0)do { if (config_debug && !(need_pages > 0)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 421, "need_pages > 0"); abort(); } } while (0);
422
423 if (remove) {
424 arena_run_split_remove(arena, chunk, run_ind, flag_dirty,
425 need_pages);
426 }
427
428 if (zero) {
429 if (flag_dirty == 0) {
430 /*
431 * The run is clean, so some pages may be zeroed (i.e.
432 * never before touched).
433 */
434 for (i = 0; i < need_pages; i++) {
435 if (arena_mapbits_unzeroed_getje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk, run_ind+i)
436 != 0)
437 arena_run_zero(chunk, run_ind+i, 1);
438 else if (config_debug) {
439 arena_run_page_validate_zeroed(chunk,
440 run_ind+i);
441 } else {
442 arena_run_page_mark_zeroed(chunk,
443 run_ind+i);
444 }
445 }
446 } else {
447 /* The run is dirty, so all pages must be zeroed. */
448 arena_run_zero(chunk, run_ind, need_pages);
449 }
450 } else {
451 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_UNDEFINED((void *)((uintptr_t)chunk +do {} while (0)
452 (run_ind << LG_PAGE)), (need_pages << LG_PAGE))do {} while (0);
453 }
454
455 /*
456 * Set the last element first, in case the run only contains one page
457 * (i.e. both statements set the same element).
458 */
459 arena_mapbits_large_setje_arena_mapbits_large_set(chunk, run_ind+need_pages-1, 0, flag_dirty);
460 arena_mapbits_large_setje_arena_mapbits_large_set(chunk, run_ind, size, flag_dirty);
461}
462
463static void
464arena_run_split_large(arena_t *arena, arena_run_t *run, size_t size, bool_Bool zero)
465{
466
467 arena_run_split_large_helper(arena, run, size, true1, zero);
468}
469
470static void
471arena_run_init_large(arena_t *arena, arena_run_t *run, size_t size, bool_Bool zero)
472{
473
474 arena_run_split_large_helper(arena, run, size, false0, zero);
475}
476
477static void
478arena_run_split_small(arena_t *arena, arena_run_t *run, size_t size,
479 size_t binind)
480{
481 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
482 size_t flag_dirty, run_ind, need_pages, i;
483
484 assert(binind != BININD_INVALID)do { if (config_debug && !(binind != ((size_t)0xffU))
) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 484, "binind != BININD_INVALID"); abort(); }
} while (0);
485
486 chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(run)((void *)((uintptr_t)(run) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
487 run_ind = (unsigned)(((uintptr_t)run - (uintptr_t)chunk) >> LG_PAGE12);
488 flag_dirty = arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind);
489 need_pages = (size >> LG_PAGE12);
490 assert(need_pages > 0)do { if (config_debug && !(need_pages > 0)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 490, "need_pages > 0"); abort(); } } while (0);
491
492 arena_run_split_remove(arena, chunk, run_ind, flag_dirty, need_pages);
493
494 /*
495 * Propagate the dirty and unzeroed flags to the allocated small run,
496 * so that arena_dalloc_bin_run() has the ability to conditionally trim
497 * clean pages.
498 */
499 arena_mapbits_small_setje_arena_mapbits_small_set(chunk, run_ind, 0, binind, flag_dirty);
500 /*
501 * The first page will always be dirtied during small run
502 * initialization, so a validation failure here would not actually
503 * cause an observable failure.
504 */
505 if (config_debug && flag_dirty == 0 && arena_mapbits_unzeroed_getje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk,
506 run_ind) == 0)
507 arena_run_page_validate_zeroed(chunk, run_ind);
508 for (i = 1; i < need_pages - 1; i++) {
509 arena_mapbits_small_setje_arena_mapbits_small_set(chunk, run_ind+i, i, binind, 0);
510 if (config_debug && flag_dirty == 0 &&
511 arena_mapbits_unzeroed_getje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk, run_ind+i) == 0)
512 arena_run_page_validate_zeroed(chunk, run_ind+i);
513 }
514 arena_mapbits_small_setje_arena_mapbits_small_set(chunk, run_ind+need_pages-1, need_pages-1,
515 binind, flag_dirty);
516 if (config_debug && flag_dirty == 0 && arena_mapbits_unzeroed_getje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk,
517 run_ind+need_pages-1) == 0)
518 arena_run_page_validate_zeroed(chunk, run_ind+need_pages-1);
519 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_UNDEFINED((void *)((uintptr_t)chunk +do {} while (0)
520 (run_ind << LG_PAGE)), (need_pages << LG_PAGE))do {} while (0);
521}
522
523static arena_chunk_t *
524arena_chunk_init_spare(arena_t *arena)
525{
526 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
527
528 assert(arena->spare != NULL)do { if (config_debug && !(arena->spare != ((void*
)0))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 528, "arena->spare != NULL"); abort(); } }
while (0);
529
530 chunk = arena->spare;
531 arena->spare = NULL((void*)0);
532
533 assert(arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk, map_bias) == 0)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_allocated_get
(chunk, je_map_bias) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 533, "arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk, map_bias) == 0"
); abort(); } } while (0);
534 assert(arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1) == 0)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_allocated_get
(chunk, je_chunk_npages-1) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 534, "arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1) == 0"
); abort(); } } while (0);
535 assert(arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, map_bias) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, je_map_bias) == je_arena_maxclass)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 536, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, map_bias) == arena_maxclass"
); abort(); } } while (0)
536 arena_maxclass)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, je_map_bias) == je_arena_maxclass)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 536, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, map_bias) == arena_maxclass"
); abort(); } } while (0);
537 assert(arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, je_chunk_npages-1) == je_arena_maxclass)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 538, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1) == arena_maxclass"
); abort(); } } while (0)
538 arena_maxclass)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, je_chunk_npages-1) == je_arena_maxclass)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 538, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1) == arena_maxclass"
); abort(); } } while (0);
539 assert(arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, map_bias) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, je_map_bias) == je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, je_chunk_npages
-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 540, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, map_bias) == arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
540 arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1))do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, je_map_bias) == je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, je_chunk_npages
-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 540, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, map_bias) == arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
541
542 return (chunk);
543}

545static arena_chunk_t *
546arena_chunk_init_hard(arena_t *arena)
547{
548 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
549 bool_Bool zero;
550 size_t unzeroed, i;
551
552 assert(arena->spare == NULL)do { if (config_debug && !(arena->spare == ((void*
)0))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 552, "arena->spare == NULL"); abort(); } }
while (0);
553
554 zero = false0;
555 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
556 chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)chunk_allocje_chunk_alloc(chunksizeje_chunksize, chunksizeje_chunksize, false0,
557 &zero, arena->dss_prec);
558 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&arena->lock);
559 if (chunk == NULL((void*)0))
560 return (NULL((void*)0));
561 if (config_stats)

567 * Claim that no pages are in use, since the header is merely overhead.
568 */

576 * the pages as zeroed iff chunk_alloc() returned a zeroed chunk.
577 */

579 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk, map_biasje_map_bias, arena_maxclassje_arena_maxclass,
580 unzeroed);
581 /*

583 * the chunk is not zeroed.
584 */
585 if (zero == false0) {
586 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_UNDEFINED((void *)arena_mapp_get(chunk,do {} while (0)
587 map_bias+1), (size_t)((uintptr_t) arena_mapp_get(chunk,do {} while (0)
588 chunk_npages-1) - (uintptr_t)arena_mapp_get(chunk,do {} while (0)
589 map_bias+1)))do {} while (0);
590 for (i = map_biasje_map_bias+1; i < chunk_npagesje_chunk_npages-1; i++)
591 arena_mapbits_unzeroed_setje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_set(chunk, i, unzeroed);
592 } else {
593 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_DEFINED((void *)arena_mapp_get(chunk,do {} while (0)
594 map_bias+1), (size_t)((uintptr_t) arena_mapp_get(chunk,do {} while (0)
595 chunk_npages-1) - (uintptr_t)arena_mapp_get(chunk,do {} while (0)
596 map_bias+1)))do {} while (0);
597 if (config_debug) {
598 for (i = map_biasje_map_bias+1; i < chunk_npagesje_chunk_npages-1; i++) {
599 assert(arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk, i) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get

); abort(); } } while (0)
600 unzeroed)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get
(chunk, i) == unzeroed)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"

602 }
603 }
604 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk, chunk_npagesje_chunk_npages-1, arena_maxclassje_arena_maxclass,
605 unzeroed);

608}

610static arena_chunk_t *
611arena_chunk_alloc(arena_t *arena)
612{
613 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
614
615 if (arena->spare != NULL((void*)0))
616 chunk = arena_chunk_init_spare(arena);
617 else {
618 chunk = arena_chunk_init_hard(arena);
619 if (chunk == NULL((void*)0))
620 return (NULL((void*)0));
621 }
622
623 /* Insert the run into the runs_avail tree. */
624 arena_avail_insert(arena, chunk, map_biasje_map_bias, chunk_npagesje_chunk_npages-map_biasje_map_bias,
625 false0, false0);
626
627 return (chunk);
628}

640 arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1))do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get

647 false0, false0);

662static arena_run_t *
663arena_run_alloc_large_helper(arena_t *arena, size_t size, bool_Bool zero)
664{
665 arena_run_t *run;
666 arena_chunk_map_t *mapelm, key;
667
668 key.bits = size | CHUNK_MAP_KEY((size_t)0x1U);
669 mapelm = arena_avail_tree_nsearch(&arena->runs_avail, &key);
670 if (mapelm != NULL((void*)0)) {
671 arena_chunk_t *run_chunk = CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(mapelm)((void *)((uintptr_t)(mapelm) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
672 size_t pageind = (((uintptr_t)mapelm -
673 (uintptr_t)run_chunk->map) / sizeof(arena_chunk_map_t))
674 + map_biasje_map_bias;
675
676 run = (arena_run_t *)((uintptr_t)run_chunk + (pageind <<
677 LG_PAGE12));
678 arena_run_split_large(arena, run, size, zero);
679 return (run);
680 }
681
682 return (NULL((void*)0));
683}
684
685static arena_run_t *
686arena_run_alloc_large(arena_t *arena, size_t size, bool_Bool zero)
687{
688 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
689 arena_run_t *run;
690
691 assert(size <= arena_maxclass)do { if (config_debug && !(size <= je_arena_maxclass
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 691, "size <= arena_maxclass"); abort(); }
} while (0);
692 assert((size & PAGE_MASK) == 0)do { if (config_debug && !((size & ((size_t)(((size_t
)(1U << 12)) - 1))) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 692, "(size & PAGE_MASK) == 0"); abort()
; } } while (0);
693
694 /* Search the arena's chunks for the lowest best fit. */
695 run = arena_run_alloc_large_helper(arena, size, zero);
696 if (run != NULL((void*)0))
697 return (run);
698
699 /*
700 * No usable runs. Create a new chunk from which to allocate the run.
701 */
702 chunk = arena_chunk_alloc(arena);
703 if (chunk != NULL((void*)0)) {
704 run = (arena_run_t *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (map_biasje_map_bias << LG_PAGE12));
705 arena_run_split_large(arena, run, size, zero);
706 return (run);
707 }
708
709 /*
710 * arena_chunk_alloc() failed, but another thread may have made
711 * sufficient memory available while this one dropped arena->lock in
712 * arena_chunk_alloc(), so search one more time.
713 */
714 return (arena_run_alloc_large_helper(arena, size, zero));
715}

741arena_run_alloc_small(arena_t *arena, size_t size, size_t binind)
742{

744 arena_run_t *run;

746 assert(size <= arena_maxclass)do { if (config_debug && !(size <= je_arena_maxclass

, "src/arena.c", 746, "size <= arena_maxclass"); abort(); }

747 assert((size & PAGE_MASK) == 0)do { if (config_debug && !((size & ((size_t)(((size_t
)(1U << 12)) - 1))) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 747, "(size & PAGE_MASK) == 0"); abort()
; } } while (0);
748 assert(binind != BININD_INVALID)do { if (config_debug && !(binind != ((size_t)0xffU))

, "src/arena.c", 748, "binind != BININD_INVALID"); abort(); }

749

751 run = arena_run_alloc_small_helper(arena, size, binind);
752 if (run != NULL((void*)0))
753 return (run);
754

756 * No usable runs. Create a new chunk from which to allocate the run.
757 */

761 arena_run_split_small(arena, run, size, binind);
762 return (run);
763 }
764
765 /*
766 * arena_chunk_alloc() failed, but another thread may have made
767 * sufficient memory available while this one dropped arena->lock in
768 * arena_chunk_alloc(), so search one more time.
769 */
770 return (arena_run_alloc_small_helper(arena, size, binind));
771}
772
773static inline void
774arena_maybe_purge(arena_t *arena)
775{
776 size_t npurgeable, threshold;
777
778 /* Don't purge if the option is disabled. */
779 if (opt_lg_dirty_multje_opt_lg_dirty_mult < 0)
780 return;
781 /* Don't purge if all dirty pages are already being purged. */
782 if (arena->ndirty <= arena->npurgatory)
783 return;
784 npurgeable = arena->ndirty - arena->npurgatory;
785 threshold = (arena->nactive >> opt_lg_dirty_multje_opt_lg_dirty_mult);
786 /*
787 * Don't purge unless the number of purgeable pages exceeds the
788 * threshold.
789 */
790 if (npurgeable <= threshold)
791 return;
792
793 arena_purge(arena, false0);
794}
795
796static arena_chunk_t *
797chunks_dirty_iter_cb(arena_chunk_tree_t *tree, arena_chunk_t *chunk, void *arg)
798{
799 size_t *ndirty = (size_t *)arg;
800
801 assert(chunk->ndirty != 0)do { if (config_debug && !(chunk->ndirty != 0)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 801, "chunk->ndirty != 0"); abort(); } } while (0);
802 *ndirty += chunk->ndirty;
803 return (NULL((void*)0));
804}
805
806static size_t
807arena_compute_npurgatory(arena_t *arena, bool_Bool all)
808{
809 size_t npurgatory, npurgeable;
810
811 /*
812 * Compute the minimum number of pages that this thread should try to
813 * purge.
814 */
815 npurgeable = arena->ndirty - arena->npurgatory;
816
817 if (all == false0) {
818 size_t threshold = (arena->nactive >> opt_lg_dirty_multje_opt_lg_dirty_mult);
819
820 npurgatory = npurgeable - threshold;
821 } else
822 npurgatory = npurgeable;
823
824 return (npurgatory);
825}

827static void
828arena_chunk_stash_dirty(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, bool_Bool all,
829 arena_chunk_mapelms_t *mapelms)
830{
831 size_t pageind, npages;
832
833 /*
834 * Temporarily allocate free dirty runs within chunk. If all is false,
835 * only operate on dirty runs that are fragments; otherwise operate on
836 * all dirty runs.
837 */
838 for (pageind = map_biasje_map_bias; pageind < chunk_npagesje_chunk_npages; pageind += npages) {
839 arena_chunk_map_t *mapelm = arena_mapp_getje_arena_mapp_get(chunk, pageind);
840 if (arena_mapbits_allocated_getje_arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk, pageind) == 0) {

, "src/arena.c", 845, "pageind + npages <= chunk_npages");
abort(); } } while (0);

(chunk, pageind) == je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind
+npages-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 847, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind) == arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind+npages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
847 arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind+npages-1))do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, pageind) == je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind
+npages-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 847, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind) == arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind+npages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
848
849 if (arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind) != 0 &&
850 (all || arena_avail_adjac(chunk, pageind,
851 npages))) {
852 arena_run_t *run = (arena_run_t *)((uintptr_t)
853 chunk + (uintptr_t)(pageind << LG_PAGE12));
854
855 arena_run_split_large(arena, run, run_size,
856 false0);
857 /* Append to list for later processing. */

))->u.ql_link.qre_prev = ((mapelm)); } while (0);

)->qlh_first)); ((mapelm))->u.ql_link.qre_prev->u.ql_link
.qre_next = ((mapelm)); (((mapelms)->qlh_first))->u.ql_link
.qre_prev = ((mapelm)); } while (0); } ((mapelms)->qlh_first
) = (((mapelm))->u.ql_link.qre_next); } while (0);
860 }
861 } else {
862 /* Skip run. */

864 npages = arena_mapbits_large_size_getje_arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk,
865 pageind) >> LG_PAGE12;
866 } else {
867 size_t binind;
868 arena_bin_info_t *bin_info;
869 arena_run_t *run = (arena_run_t *)((uintptr_t)
870 chunk + (uintptr_t)(pageind << LG_PAGE12));

884
885static size_t
886arena_chunk_purge_stashed(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk,
887 arena_chunk_mapelms_t *mapelms)
888{
889 size_t npurged, pageind, npages, nmadvise;
890 arena_chunk_map_t *mapelm;
891
892 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
893 if (config_stats)
894 nmadvise = 0;
895 npurged = 0;
896 ql_foreach(mapelm, mapelms, u.ql_link)for (((mapelm)) = (((mapelms)->qlh_first)); ((mapelm)) != (
(void*)0); ((mapelm)) = ((((mapelm))->u.ql_link.qre_next !=
(((mapelms)->qlh_first))) ? ((mapelm))->u.ql_link.qre_next
: ((void*)0))) {
897 bool_Bool unzeroed;
898 size_t flag_unzeroed, i;
899
900 pageind = (((uintptr_t)mapelm - (uintptr_t)chunk->map) /
901 sizeof(arena_chunk_map_t)) + map_biasje_map_bias;
902 npages = arena_mapbits_large_size_getje_arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, pageind) >>
903 LG_PAGE12;
904 assert(pageind + npages <= chunk_npages)do { if (config_debug && !(pageind + npages <= je_chunk_npages
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 904, "pageind + npages <= chunk_npages");
abort(); } } while (0);
905 unzeroed = pages_purgeje_pages_purge((void *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (pageind <<
906 LG_PAGE12)), (npages << LG_PAGE12));
907 flag_unzeroed = unzeroed ? CHUNK_MAP_UNZEROED((size_t)0x4U) : 0;
908 /*
909 * Set the unzeroed flag for all pages, now that pages_purge()
910 * has returned whether the pages were zeroed as a side effect
911 * of purging. This chunk map modification is safe even though
912 * the arena mutex isn't currently owned by this thread,
913 * because the run is marked as allocated, thus protecting it
914 * from being modified by any other thread. As long as these
915 * writes don't perturb the first and last elements'
916 * CHUNK_MAP_ALLOCATED bits, behavior is well defined.
917 */
918 for (i = 0; i < npages; i++) {
919 arena_mapbits_unzeroed_setje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_set(chunk, pageind+i,
920 flag_unzeroed);
921 }
922 npurged += npages;
923 if (config_stats)
924 nmadvise++;
925 }
926 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&arena->lock);
927 if (config_stats)
928 arena->stats.nmadvise += nmadvise;
929
930 return (npurged);
931}
932
933static void
934arena_chunk_unstash_purged(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk,
935 arena_chunk_mapelms_t *mapelms)
936{
937 arena_chunk_map_t *mapelm;
938 size_t pageind;
939
940 /* Deallocate runs. */
941 for (mapelm = ql_first(mapelms)((mapelms)->qlh_first); mapelm != NULL((void*)0);
942 mapelm = ql_first(mapelms)((mapelms)->qlh_first)) {
943 arena_run_t *run;
944
945 pageind = (((uintptr_t)mapelm - (uintptr_t)chunk->map) /
946 sizeof(arena_chunk_map_t)) + map_biasje_map_bias;
947 run = (arena_run_t *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (uintptr_t)(pageind <<
948 LG_PAGE12));
949 ql_remove(mapelms, mapelm, u.ql_link)do { if (((mapelms)->qlh_first) == (mapelm)) { ((mapelms)->
qlh_first) = ((((mapelms)->qlh_first))->u.ql_link.qre_next
); } if (((mapelms)->qlh_first) != (mapelm)) { do { ((mapelm
))->u.ql_link.qre_prev->u.ql_link.qre_next = ((mapelm))
->u.ql_link.qre_next; ((mapelm))->u.ql_link.qre_next->
u.ql_link.qre_prev = ((mapelm))->u.ql_link.qre_prev; ((mapelm
))->u.ql_link.qre_next = ((mapelm)); ((mapelm))->u.ql_link
.qre_prev = ((mapelm)); } while (0); } else { ((mapelms)->
qlh_first) = ((void*)0); } } while (0);
950 arena_run_dalloc(arena, run, false0, true1);
951 }
952}
953
954static inline size_t
955arena_chunk_purge(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, bool_Bool all)
956{
957 size_t npurged;
958 arena_chunk_mapelms_t mapelms;
959
960 ql_new(&mapelms)do { (&mapelms)->qlh_first = ((void*)0); } while (0);
961
962 /*
963 * If chunk is the spare, temporarily re-allocate it, 1) so that its
964 * run is reinserted into runs_avail, and 2) so that it cannot be
965 * completely discarded by another thread while arena->lock is dropped
966 * by this thread. Note that the arena_run_dalloc() call will
967 * implicitly deallocate the chunk, so no explicit action is required
968 * in this function to deallocate the chunk.
969 *
970 * Note that once a chunk contains dirty pages, it cannot again contain
971 * a single run unless 1) it is a dirty run, or 2) this function purges
972 * dirty pages and causes the transition to a single clean run. Thus
973 * (chunk == arena->spare) is possible, but it is not possible for
974 * this function to be called on the spare unless it contains a dirty
975 * run.
976 */
977 if (chunk == arena->spare) {
978 assert(arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, map_bias) != 0)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, je_map_bias) != 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 978, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, map_bias) != 0"
); abort(); } } while (0);
979 assert(arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1) != 0)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, je_chunk_npages-1) != 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 979, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, chunk_npages-1) != 0"
); abort(); } } while (0);
980
981 arena_chunk_alloc(arena);
982 }
983
984 if (config_stats)
985 arena->stats.purged += chunk->ndirty;
986
987 /*
988 * Operate on all dirty runs if there is no clean/dirty run
989 * fragmentation.
990 */
991 if (chunk->nruns_adjac == 0)
992 all = true1;
993
994 arena_chunk_stash_dirty(arena, chunk, all, &mapelms);
995 npurged = arena_chunk_purge_stashed(arena, chunk, &mapelms);
996 arena_chunk_unstash_purged(arena, chunk, &mapelms);
997
998 return (npurged);
999}
1000
1001static void
1002arena_purge(arena_t *arena, bool_Bool all)
1003{
1004 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
1005 size_t npurgatory;
1006 if (config_debug) {
1007 size_t ndirty = 0;
1008
1009 arena_chunk_dirty_iter(&arena->chunks_dirty, NULL((void*)0),
1010 chunks_dirty_iter_cb, (void *)&ndirty);
1011 assert(ndirty == arena->ndirty)do { if (config_debug && !(ndirty == arena->ndirty
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1011, "ndirty == arena->ndirty"); abort()
; } } while (0);
1012 }
1013 assert(arena->ndirty > arena->npurgatory || all)do { if (config_debug && !(arena->ndirty > arena
->npurgatory || all)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1013, "arena->ndirty > arena->npurgatory || all"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1014 assert((arena->nactive >> opt_lg_dirty_mult) < (arena->ndirty -do { if (config_debug && !((arena->nactive >>
je_opt_lg_dirty_mult) < (arena->ndirty - arena->npurgatory
) || all)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1015, "(arena->nactive >> opt_lg_dirty_mult) < (arena->ndirty - arena->npurgatory) || all"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1015 arena->npurgatory) || all)do { if (config_debug && !((arena->nactive >>
je_opt_lg_dirty_mult) < (arena->ndirty - arena->npurgatory
) || all)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1015, "(arena->nactive >> opt_lg_dirty_mult) < (arena->ndirty - arena->npurgatory) || all"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1016
1017 if (config_stats)
1018 arena->stats.npurge++;
1019
1020 /*
1021 * Add the minimum number of pages this thread should try to purge to
1022 * arena->npurgatory. This will keep multiple threads from racing to
1023 * reduce ndirty below the threshold.
1024 */
1025 npurgatory = arena_compute_npurgatory(arena, all);
1026 arena->npurgatory += npurgatory;
1027
1028 while (npurgatory > 0) {
1029 size_t npurgeable, npurged, nunpurged;
1030
1031 /* Get next chunk with dirty pages. */
1032 chunk = arena_chunk_dirty_first(&arena->chunks_dirty);
1033 if (chunk == NULL((void*)0)) {
1034 /*
1035 * This thread was unable to purge as many pages as
1036 * originally intended, due to races with other threads
1037 * that either did some of the purging work, or re-used
1038 * dirty pages.
1039 */
1040 arena->npurgatory -= npurgatory;
1041 return;
1042 }
1043 npurgeable = chunk->ndirty;
1044 assert(npurgeable != 0)do { if (config_debug && !(npurgeable != 0)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 1044, "npurgeable != 0"); abort(); } } while (0);
1045
1046 if (npurgeable > npurgatory && chunk->nruns_adjac == 0) {
1047 /*
1048 * This thread will purge all the dirty pages in chunk,
1049 * so set npurgatory to reflect this thread's intent to
1050 * purge the pages. This tends to reduce the chances
1051 * of the following scenario:
1052 *
1053 * 1) This thread sets arena->npurgatory such that
1054 * (arena->ndirty - arena->npurgatory) is at the
1055 * threshold.
1056 * 2) This thread drops arena->lock.
1057 * 3) Another thread causes one or more pages to be
1058 * dirtied, and immediately determines that it must
1059 * purge dirty pages.
1060 *
1061 * If this scenario *does* play out, that's okay,
1062 * because all of the purging work being done really
1063 * needs to happen.
1064 */
1065 arena->npurgatory += npurgeable - npurgatory;
1066 npurgatory = npurgeable;
1067 }
1068
1069 /*
1070 * Keep track of how many pages are purgeable, versus how many
1071 * actually get purged, and adjust counters accordingly.
1072 */
1073 arena->npurgatory -= npurgeable;
1074 npurgatory -= npurgeable;
1075 npurged = arena_chunk_purge(arena, chunk, all);
1076 nunpurged = npurgeable - npurged;
1077 arena->npurgatory += nunpurged;
1078 npurgatory += nunpurged;
1079 }
1080}
1081
1082void
1083arena_purge_allje_arena_purge_all(arena_t *arena)
1084{
1085
1086 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&arena->lock);
1087 arena_purge(arena, true1);
1088 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
1089}

1091static void
1092arena_run_coalesce(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, size_t *p_size,
1093 size_t *p_run_ind, size_t *p_run_pages, size_t flag_dirty)
1094{
1095 size_t size = *p_size;
1096 size_t run_ind = *p_run_ind;
1097 size_t run_pages = *p_run_pages;
1098
1099 /* Try to coalesce forward. */
1100 if (run_ind + run_pages < chunk_npagesje_chunk_npages &&
1101 arena_mapbits_allocated_getje_arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages) == 0 &&
1102 arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages) == flag_dirty) {
1103 size_t nrun_size = arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_getje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk,
1104 run_ind+run_pages);
1105 size_t nrun_pages = nrun_size >> LG_PAGE12;
1106
1107 /*
1108 * Remove successor from runs_avail; the coalesced run is
1109 * inserted later.
1110 */
1111 assert(arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk,do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == nrun_size)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 1112, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == nrun_size"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1112 run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == nrun_size)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == nrun_size)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 1112, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == nrun_size"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1113 assert(arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk,do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == flag_dirty)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 1114, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == flag_dirty"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1114 run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == flag_dirty)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == flag_dirty)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 1114, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages+nrun_pages-1) == flag_dirty"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1115 arena_avail_remove(arena, chunk, run_ind+run_pages, nrun_pages,
1116 false0, true1);
1117
1118 size += nrun_size;
1119 run_pages += nrun_pages;
1120
1121 arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_set(chunk, run_ind, size);
1122 arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_set(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1,
1123 size);
1124 }
1125
1126 /* Try to coalesce backward. */
1127 if (run_ind > map_biasje_map_bias && arena_mapbits_allocated_getje_arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk,
1128 run_ind-1) == 0 && arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind-1) ==
1129 flag_dirty) {
1130 size_t prun_size = arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_getje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk,
1131 run_ind-1);
1132 size_t prun_pages = prun_size >> LG_PAGE12;
1133
1134 run_ind -= prun_pages;
1135
1136 /*
1137 * Remove predecessor from runs_avail; the coalesced run is
1138 * inserted later.
1139 */
1140 assert(arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, run_ind) == prun_size)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1141, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind) == prun_size"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1141 prun_size)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, run_ind) == prun_size)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1141, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind) == prun_size"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1142 assert(arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) == flag_dirty)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind) == flag_dirty)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1142, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) == flag_dirty"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1143 arena_avail_remove(arena, chunk, run_ind, prun_pages, true1,
1144 false0);
1145
1146 size += prun_size;
1147 run_pages += prun_pages;
1148
1149 arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_set(chunk, run_ind, size);
1150 arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_set(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1,
1151 size);
1152 }
1153
1154 *p_size = size;
1155 *p_run_ind = run_ind;
1156 *p_run_pages = run_pages;
1157}
1158
1159static void
1160arena_run_dalloc(arena_t *arena, arena_run_t *run, bool_Bool dirty, bool_Bool cleaned)
1161{
1162 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
1163 size_t size, run_ind, run_pages, flag_dirty;
1164
1165 chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(run)((void *)((uintptr_t)(run) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
1166 run_ind = (size_t)(((uintptr_t)run - (uintptr_t)chunk) >> LG_PAGE12);
1167 assert(run_ind >= map_bias)do { if (config_debug && !(run_ind >= je_map_bias)
) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1167, "run_ind >= map_bias"); abort(); } }
while (0);
1168 assert(run_ind < chunk_npages)do { if (config_debug && !(run_ind < je_chunk_npages
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1168, "run_ind < chunk_npages"); abort();
} } while (0);
1169 if (arena_mapbits_large_getje_arena_mapbits_large_get(chunk, run_ind) != 0) {
1170 size = arena_mapbits_large_size_getje_arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, run_ind);
1171 assert(size == PAGE ||do { if (config_debug && !(size == ((size_t)(1U <<
12)) || je_arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, run_ind+(size
>>12)-1) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1173, "size == PAGE || arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, run_ind+(size>>LG_PAGE)-1) == 0"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1172 arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk,do { if (config_debug && !(size == ((size_t)(1U <<
12)) || je_arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, run_ind+(size
>>12)-1) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1173, "size == PAGE || arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, run_ind+(size>>LG_PAGE)-1) == 0"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1173 run_ind+(size>>LG_PAGE)-1) == 0)do { if (config_debug && !(size == ((size_t)(1U <<
12)) || je_arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, run_ind+(size
>>12)-1) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1173, "size == PAGE || arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, run_ind+(size>>LG_PAGE)-1) == 0"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1174 } else {
1175 size_t binind = arena_bin_indexje_arena_bin_index(arena, run->bin);
1176 arena_bin_info_t *bin_info = &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind];
1177 size = bin_info->run_size;
1178 }
1179 run_pages = (size >> LG_PAGE12);
1180 arena_cactive_update(arena, 0, run_pages);
1181 arena->nactive -= run_pages;
1182
1183 /*
1184 * The run is dirty if the caller claims to have dirtied it, as well as
1185 * if it was already dirty before being allocated and the caller
1186 * doesn't claim to have cleaned it.
1187 */
1188 assert(arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind) == je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind
+run_pages-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1189, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) == arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1189 arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1))do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind) == je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind
+run_pages-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1189, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) == arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1190 if (cleaned == false0 && arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) != 0)
1191 dirty = true1;
1192 flag_dirty = dirty ? CHUNK_MAP_DIRTY((size_t)0x8U) : 0;
1193
1194 /* Mark pages as unallocated in the chunk map. */
1195 if (dirty) {
1196 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk, run_ind, size,
1197 CHUNK_MAP_DIRTY((size_t)0x8U));
1198 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1, size,
1199 CHUNK_MAP_DIRTY((size_t)0x8U));
1200 } else {
1201 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk, run_ind, size,
1202 arena_mapbits_unzeroed_getje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk, run_ind));
1203 arena_mapbits_unallocated_setje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_set(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1, size,
1204 arena_mapbits_unzeroed_getje_arena_mapbits_unzeroed_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1));
1205 }
1206
1207 arena_run_coalesce(arena, chunk, &size, &run_ind, &run_pages,
1208 flag_dirty);
1209
1210 /* Insert into runs_avail, now that coalescing is complete. */
1211 assert(arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, run_ind) == je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk
, run_ind+run_pages-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1212, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind) == arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1212 arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1))do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get
(chunk, run_ind) == je_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk
, run_ind+run_pages-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1212, "arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind) == arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1213 assert(arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) ==do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind) == je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind
+run_pages-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1214, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) == arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0)
1214 arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1))do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get
(chunk, run_ind) == je_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind
+run_pages-1))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1214, "arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind) == arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, run_ind+run_pages-1)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1215 arena_avail_insert(arena, chunk, run_ind, run_pages, true1, true1);
1216
1217 /* Deallocate chunk if it is now completely unused. */
1218 if (size == arena_maxclassje_arena_maxclass) {
1219 assert(run_ind == map_bias)do { if (config_debug && !(run_ind == je_map_bias)) {
je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1219, "run_ind == map_bias"); abort(); } } while
(0);
1220 assert(run_pages == (arena_maxclass >> LG_PAGE))do { if (config_debug && !(run_pages == (je_arena_maxclass
>> 12))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1220, "run_pages == (arena_maxclass >> LG_PAGE)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
1221 arena_chunk_dealloc(arena, chunk);
1222 }
1223
1224 /*
1225 * It is okay to do dirty page processing here even if the chunk was
1226 * deallocated above, since in that case it is the spare. Waiting
1227 * until after possible chunk deallocation to do dirty processing
1228 * allows for an old spare to be fully deallocated, thus decreasing the
1229 * chances of spuriously crossing the dirty page purging threshold.
1230 */
1231 if (dirty)
1232 arena_maybe_purge(arena);
1233}

1235static void

1238{

1253
1254 if (config_debug) {
1255 UNUSED__attribute__((unused)) size_t tail_npages = newsize >> LG_PAGE12;
1256 assert(arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk,do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_large_size_get

1257 pageind+head_npages+tail_npages-1) == 0)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_large_size_get

1288 assert(arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk,do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_mapbits_large_size_get

1300static arena_run_t *
1301arena_bin_runs_first(arena_bin_t *bin)

1309 chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(mapelm)((void *)((uintptr_t)(mapelm) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
1310 pageind = ((((uintptr_t)mapelm - (uintptr_t)chunk->map) /
1311 sizeof(arena_chunk_map_t))) + map_biasje_map_bias;
1312 run = (arena_run_t *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (uintptr_t)((pageind -
1313 arena_mapbits_small_runind_getje_arena_mapbits_small_runind_get(chunk, pageind)) <<
1314 LG_PAGE12));

1345static arena_run_t *
1346arena_bin_nonfull_run_tryget(arena_bin_t *bin)
1347{
1348 arena_run_t *run = arena_bin_runs_first(bin);
1349 if (run != NULL((void*)0)) {
1350 arena_bin_runs_remove(bin, run);
1351 if (config_stats)
1352 bin->stats.reruns++;
1353 }
1354 return (run);
1355}
1356
1357static arena_run_t *
1358arena_bin_nonfull_run_get(arena_t *arena, arena_bin_t *bin)
1359{
1360 arena_run_t *run;
1361 size_t binind;
1362 arena_bin_info_t *bin_info;
1363
1364 /* Look for a usable run. */
1365 run = arena_bin_nonfull_run_tryget(bin);
1366 if (run != NULL((void*)0))
1367 return (run);
1368 /* No existing runs have any space available. */
1369
1370 binind = arena_bin_indexje_arena_bin_index(arena, bin);
1371 bin_info = &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind];
1372
1373 /* Allocate a new run. */
1374 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&bin->lock);
1375 /******************************/
1376 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&arena->lock);
1377 run = arena_run_alloc_small(arena, bin_info->run_size, binind);
1378 if (run != NULL((void*)0)) {
1379 bitmap_t *bitmap = (bitmap_t *)((uintptr_t)run +
1380 (uintptr_t)bin_info->bitmap_offset);
1381
1382 /* Initialize run internals. */
1383 run->bin = bin;
1384 run->nextind = 0;
1385 run->nfree = bin_info->nregs;
1386 bitmap_initje_bitmap_init(bitmap, &bin_info->bitmap_info);
1387 }
1388 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
1389 /********************************/
1390 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&bin->lock);
1391 if (run != NULL((void*)0)) {
1392 if (config_stats) {
1393 bin->stats.nruns++;
1394 bin->stats.curruns++;
1395 }
1396 return (run);
1397 }
1398
1399 /*
1400 * arena_run_alloc_small() failed, but another thread may have made
1401 * sufficient memory available while this one dropped bin->lock above,
1402 * so search one more time.
1403 */
1404 run = arena_bin_nonfull_run_tryget(bin);
1405 if (run != NULL((void*)0))
1406 return (run);
1407
1408 return (NULL((void*)0));
1409}
1410
1411/* Re-fill bin->runcur, then call arena_run_reg_alloc(). */
1412static void *
1413arena_bin_malloc_hard(arena_t *arena, arena_bin_t *bin)
1414{
1415 void *ret;
1416 size_t binind;
1417 arena_bin_info_t *bin_info;
1418 arena_run_t *run;
1419
1420 binind = arena_bin_indexje_arena_bin_index(arena, bin);
1421 bin_info = &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind];
1422 bin->runcur = NULL((void*)0);
1423 run = arena_bin_nonfull_run_get(arena, bin);
1424 if (bin->runcur != NULL((void*)0) && bin->runcur->nfree > 0) {
1425 /*
1426 * Another thread updated runcur while this one ran without the
1427 * bin lock in arena_bin_nonfull_run_get().
1428 */
1429 assert(bin->runcur->nfree > 0)do { if (config_debug && !(bin->runcur->nfree >
0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1429, "bin->runcur->nfree > 0"); abort
(); } } while (0);
1430 ret = arena_run_reg_alloc(bin->runcur, bin_info);
1431 if (run != NULL((void*)0)) {
1432 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
1433
1434 /*
1435 * arena_run_alloc_small() may have allocated run, or
1436 * it may have pulled run from the bin's run tree.
1437 * Therefore it is unsafe to make any assumptions about
1438 * how run has previously been used, and
1439 * arena_bin_lower_run() must be called, as if a region
1440 * were just deallocated from the run.
1441 */
1442 chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(run)((void *)((uintptr_t)(run) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
1443 if (run->nfree == bin_info->nregs)
1444 arena_dalloc_bin_run(arena, chunk, run, bin);
1445 else
1446 arena_bin_lower_run(arena, chunk, run, bin);
1447 }
1448 return (ret);
1449 }
1450
1451 if (run == NULL((void*)0))
1452 return (NULL((void*)0));
1453
1454 bin->runcur = run;
1455
1456 assert(bin->runcur->nfree > 0)do { if (config_debug && !(bin->runcur->nfree >
0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1456, "bin->runcur->nfree > 0"); abort
(); } } while (0);
1457
1458 return (arena_run_reg_alloc(bin->runcur, bin_info));
1459}

1461void
1462arena_tcache_fill_smallje_arena_tcache_fill_small(arena_t *arena, tcache_bin_t *tbin, size_t binind,
1463 uint64_t prof_accumbytes)
1464{
1465 unsigned i, nfill;
1466 arena_bin_t *bin;
1467 arena_run_t *run;
1468 void *ptr;
1469
1470 assert(tbin->ncached == 0)do { if (config_debug && !(tbin->ncached == 0)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 1470, "tbin->ncached == 0"); abort(); } } while (0);
1471
1472 if (config_prof && arena_prof_accumje_arena_prof_accum(arena, prof_accumbytes))
1473 prof_idumpje_prof_idump();
1474 bin = &arena->bins[binind];
1475 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&bin->lock);
1476 for (i = 0, nfill = (tcache_bin_infoje_tcache_bin_info[binind].ncached_max >>
1477 tbin->lg_fill_div); i < nfill; i++) {
1478 if ((run = bin->runcur) != NULL((void*)0) && run->nfree > 0)
1479 ptr = arena_run_reg_alloc(run, &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind]);
1480 else
1481 ptr = arena_bin_malloc_hard(arena, bin);
1482 if (ptr == NULL((void*)0))
1483 break;
1484 if (config_fill && opt_junkje_opt_junk) {
1485 arena_alloc_junk_smallje_arena_alloc_junk_small(ptr, &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind],
1486 true1);
1487 }
1488 /* Insert such that low regions get used first. */
1489 tbin->avail[nfill - 1 - i] = ptr;
1490 }
1491 if (config_stats) {
1492 bin->stats.allocated += i * arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind].reg_size;
1493 bin->stats.nmalloc += i;
1494 bin->stats.nrequests += tbin->tstats.nrequests;
1495 bin->stats.nfills++;
1496 tbin->tstats.nrequests = 0;
1497 }
1498 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&bin->lock);
1499 tbin->ncached = i;
1500}

1502void
1503arena_alloc_junk_smallje_arena_alloc_junk_small(void *ptr, arena_bin_info_t *bin_info, bool_Bool zero)
1504{
1505
1506 if (zero) {
1507 size_t redzone_size = bin_info->redzone_size;
1508 memset((void *)((uintptr_t)ptr - redzone_size), 0xa5,
1509 redzone_size);
1510 memset((void *)((uintptr_t)ptr + bin_info->reg_size), 0xa5,
1511 redzone_size);
1512 } else {
1513 memset((void *)((uintptr_t)ptr - bin_info->redzone_size), 0xa5,
1514 bin_info->reg_interval);
1515 }
1516}

1538static void
1539arena_redzones_validate(void *ptr, arena_bin_info_t *bin_info, bool_Bool reset)
1540{
1541 size_t size = bin_info->reg_size;
1542 size_t redzone_size = bin_info->redzone_size;
1543 size_t i;
1544 bool_Bool error = false0;
1545
1546 for (i = 1; i <= redzone_size; i++) {
1547 uint8_t *byte = (uint8_t *)((uintptr_t)ptr - i);
1548 if (*byte != 0xa5) {
1549 error = true1;
1550 arena_redzone_corruptionje_arena_redzone_corruption(ptr, size, false0, i, *byte);
1551 if (reset)
1552 *byte = 0xa5;
1553 }
1554 }
1555 for (i = 0; i < redzone_size; i++) {
1556 uint8_t *byte = (uint8_t *)((uintptr_t)ptr + size + i);
1557 if (*byte != 0xa5) {
1558 error = true1;
1559 arena_redzone_corruptionje_arena_redzone_corruption(ptr, size, true1, i, *byte);
1560 if (reset)
1561 *byte = 0xa5;
1562 }
1563 }
1564 if (opt_abortje_opt_abort && error)
1565 abort();
1566}

1603void *
1604arena_malloc_smallje_arena_malloc_small(arena_t *arena, size_t size, bool_Bool zero)
1605{
1606 void *ret;
1607 arena_bin_t *bin;
1608 arena_run_t *run;
1609 size_t binind;
1610
1611 binind = SMALL_SIZE2BIN(size)(je_small_size2bin[(size-1) >> 3]);
1612 assert(binind < NBINS)do { if (config_debug && !(binind < 28)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 1612, "binind < NBINS"); abort(); } } while (0);
1613 bin = &arena->bins[binind];
1614 size = arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind].reg_size;
1615
1616 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&bin->lock);
1617 if ((run = bin->runcur) != NULL((void*)0) && run->nfree > 0)
1618 ret = arena_run_reg_alloc(run, &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind]);
1619 else
1620 ret = arena_bin_malloc_hard(arena, bin);
1621
1622 if (ret == NULL((void*)0)) {
1623 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&bin->lock);
1624 return (NULL((void*)0));
1625 }
1626
1627 if (config_stats) {
1628 bin->stats.allocated += size;
1629 bin->stats.nmalloc++;
1630 bin->stats.nrequests++;
1631 }
1632 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&bin->lock);
1633 if (config_prof && isthreaded1 == false0 && arena_prof_accumje_arena_prof_accum(arena, size))
1634 prof_idumpje_prof_idump();
1635
1636 if (zero == false0) {
1637 if (config_fill) {
1638 if (opt_junkje_opt_junk) {
1639 arena_alloc_junk_smallje_arena_alloc_junk_small(ret,
1640 &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind], false0);
1641 } else if (opt_zeroje_opt_zero)
1642 memset(ret, 0, size);
1643 }
1644 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_UNDEFINED(ret, size)do {} while (0);
1645 } else {
1646 if (config_fill && opt_junkje_opt_junk) {
1647 arena_alloc_junk_smallje_arena_alloc_junk_small(ret, &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind],
1648 true1);
1649 }
1650 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_UNDEFINED(ret, size)do {} while (0);
1651 memset(ret, 0, size);
1652 }
1653
1654 return (ret);
1655}

1657void *
1658arena_malloc_largeje_arena_malloc_large(arena_t *arena, size_t size, bool_Bool zero)
1659{
1660 void *ret;
1661 UNUSED__attribute__((unused)) bool_Bool idump;
1662
1663 /* Large allocation. */
1664 size = PAGE_CEILING(size)(((size) + ((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1))) & ~
((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1)));
1665 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&arena->lock);
1666 ret = (void *)arena_run_alloc_large(arena, size, zero);
1667 if (ret == NULL((void*)0)) {
1668 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
1669 return (NULL((void*)0));
1670 }
1671 if (config_stats) {
1672 arena->stats.nmalloc_large++;
1673 arena->stats.nrequests_large++;
1674 arena->stats.allocated_large += size;
1675 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].nmalloc++;
1676 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].nrequests++;
1677 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].curruns++;
1678 }
1679 if (config_prof)
1680 idump = arena_prof_accum_lockedje_arena_prof_accum_locked(arena, size);
1681 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
1682 if (config_prof && idump)
1683 prof_idumpje_prof_idump();
1684
1685 if (zero == false0) {
1686 if (config_fill) {
1687 if (opt_junkje_opt_junk)
1688 memset(ret, 0xa5, size);
1689 else if (opt_zeroje_opt_zero)
1690 memset(ret, 0, size);
1691 }
1692 }
1693
1694 return (ret);
1695}

1697/* Only handles large allocations that require more than page alignment. */
1698void *
1699arena_pallocje_arena_palloc(arena_t *arena, size_t size, size_t alignment, bool_Bool zero)
1700{
1701 void *ret;
1702 size_t alloc_size, leadsize, trailsize;
1703 arena_run_t *run;
1704 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
1705
1706 assert((size & PAGE_MASK) == 0)do { if (config_debug && !((size & ((size_t)(((size_t
)(1U << 12)) - 1))) == 0)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1706, "(size & PAGE_MASK) == 0"); abort(
); } } while (0);
1707
1708 alignment = PAGE_CEILING(alignment)(((alignment) + ((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1))) &
~((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1)));
1709 alloc_size = size + alignment - PAGE((size_t)(1U << 12));
1710
1711 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&arena->lock);
1712 run = arena_run_alloc_large(arena, alloc_size, false0);
1713 if (run == NULL((void*)0)) {
1714 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
1715 return (NULL((void*)0));
1716 }
1717 chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(run)((void *)((uintptr_t)(run) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
1718
1719 leadsize = ALIGNMENT_CEILING((uintptr_t)run, alignment)((((uintptr_t)run) + (alignment - 1)) & (-(alignment))) -
1720 (uintptr_t)run;
1721 assert(alloc_size >= leadsize + size)do { if (config_debug && !(alloc_size >= leadsize +
size)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 1721, "alloc_size >= leadsize + size"); abort
(); } } while (0);
1722 trailsize = alloc_size - leadsize - size;
1723 ret = (void *)((uintptr_t)run + leadsize);
1724 if (leadsize != 0) {
1725 arena_run_trim_head(arena, chunk, run, alloc_size, alloc_size -
1726 leadsize);
1727 }
1728 if (trailsize != 0) {
1729 arena_run_trim_tail(arena, chunk, ret, size + trailsize, size,
1730 false0);
1731 }
1732 arena_run_init_large(arena, (arena_run_t *)ret, size, zero);
1733
1734 if (config_stats) {
1735 arena->stats.nmalloc_large++;
1736 arena->stats.nrequests_large++;
1737 arena->stats.allocated_large += size;
1738 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].nmalloc++;
1739 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].nrequests++;
1740 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].curruns++;
1741 }
1742 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
1743
1744 if (config_fill && zero == false0) {
1745 if (opt_junkje_opt_junk)
1746 memset(ret, 0xa5, size);
1747 else if (opt_zeroje_opt_zero)
1748 memset(ret, 0, size);
1749 }
1750 return (ret);
1751}

1776static void
1777arena_dissociate_bin_run(arena_chunk_t *chunk, arena_run_t *run,
1778 arena_bin_t *bin)
1779{
1780
1781 /* Dissociate run from bin. */
1782 if (run == bin->runcur)
1783 bin->runcur = NULL((void*)0);
1784 else {
1785 size_t binind = arena_bin_indexje_arena_bin_index(chunk->arena, bin);
1786 arena_bin_info_t *bin_info = &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind];
1787
1788 if (bin_info->nregs != 1) {
1789 /*
1790 * This block's conditional is necessary because if the
1791 * run only contains one region, then it never gets
1792 * inserted into the non-full runs tree.
1793 */
1794 arena_bin_runs_remove(bin, run);
1795 }
1796 }
1797}

1849
1850static void
1851arena_bin_lower_run(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, arena_run_t *run,
1852 arena_bin_t *bin)
1853{
1854
1855 /*
1856 * Make sure that if bin->runcur is non-NULL, it refers to the lowest
1857 * non-full run. It is okay to NULL runcur out rather than proactively
1858 * keeping it pointing at the lowest non-full run.
1859 */
1860 if ((uintptr_t)run < (uintptr_t)bin->runcur) {
1861 /* Switch runcur. */
1862 if (bin->runcur->nfree > 0)
1863 arena_bin_runs_insert(bin, bin->runcur);
1864 bin->runcur = run;
1865 if (config_stats)
1866 bin->stats.reruns++;
1867 } else
1868 arena_bin_runs_insert(bin, run);
1869}

1871void
1872arena_dalloc_bin_lockedje_arena_dalloc_bin_locked(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, void *ptr,
1873 arena_chunk_map_t *mapelm)
1874{
1875 size_t pageind;
1876 arena_run_t *run;
1877 arena_bin_t *bin;
1878 arena_bin_info_t *bin_info;
1879 size_t size, binind;
1880
1881 pageind = ((uintptr_t)ptr - (uintptr_t)chunk) >> LG_PAGE12;
1882 run = (arena_run_t *)((uintptr_t)chunk + (uintptr_t)((pageind -
1883 arena_mapbits_small_runind_getje_arena_mapbits_small_runind_get(chunk, pageind)) << LG_PAGE12));
1884 bin = run->bin;
1885 binind = arena_ptr_small_binind_getje_arena_ptr_small_binind_get(ptr, mapelm->bits);
1886 bin_info = &arena_bin_infoje_arena_bin_info[binind];
1887 if (config_fill || config_stats)
1888 size = bin_info->reg_size;
1889
1890 if (config_fill && opt_junkje_opt_junk)
1891 arena_dalloc_junk_smallje_arena_dalloc_junk_small(ptr, bin_info);
1892
1893 arena_run_reg_dalloc(run, ptr);
1894 if (run->nfree == bin_info->nregs) {
1895 arena_dissociate_bin_run(chunk, run, bin);
1896 arena_dalloc_bin_run(arena, chunk, run, bin);
1897 } else if (run->nfree == 1 && run != bin->runcur)
1898 arena_bin_lower_run(arena, chunk, run, bin);
1899
1900 if (config_stats) {
1901 bin->stats.allocated -= size;
1902 bin->stats.ndalloc++;
1903 }
1904}

1954void

1956{

1965 arena->stats.allocated_large -= usize;
1966 arena->stats.lstats[(usize >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].ndalloc++;
1967 arena->stats.lstats[(usize >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].curruns--;
1968 }
1969 }
1970
1971 arena_run_dalloc(arena, (arena_run_t *)ptr, true1, false0);
1972}

1983static void
1984arena_ralloc_large_shrink(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, void *ptr,

2013static bool_Bool
2014arena_ralloc_large_grow(arena_t *arena, arena_chunk_t *chunk, void *ptr,
2015 size_t oldsize, size_t size, size_t extra, bool_Bool zero)
2016{
2017 size_t pageind = ((uintptr_t)ptr - (uintptr_t)chunk) >> LG_PAGE12;
2018 size_t npages = oldsize >> LG_PAGE12;
2019 size_t followsize;
2020
2021 assert(oldsize == arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, pageind))do { if (config_debug && !(oldsize == je_arena_mapbits_large_size_get
(chunk, pageind))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 2021, "oldsize == arena_mapbits_large_size_get(chunk, pageind)"
); abort(); } } while (0);
2022
2023 /* Try to extend the run. */
2024 assert(size + extra > oldsize)do { if (config_debug && !(size + extra > oldsize)
) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 2024, "size + extra > oldsize"); abort();
} } while (0);
2025 malloc_mutex_lockje_malloc_mutex_lock(&arena->lock);
2026 if (pageind + npages < chunk_npagesje_chunk_npages &&
2027 arena_mapbits_allocated_getje_arena_mapbits_allocated_get(chunk, pageind+npages) == 0 &&
2028 (followsize = arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_getje_arena_mapbits_unallocated_size_get(chunk,
2029 pageind+npages)) >= size - oldsize) {
2030 /*
2031 * The next run is available and sufficiently large. Split the
2032 * following run, then merge the first part with the existing
2033 * allocation.
2034 */
2035 size_t flag_dirty;
2036 size_t splitsize = (oldsize + followsize <= size + extra)
2037 ? followsize : size + extra - oldsize;
2038 arena_run_split_large(arena, (arena_run_t *)((uintptr_t)chunk +
2039 ((pageind+npages) << LG_PAGE12)), splitsize, zero);
2040
2041 size = oldsize + splitsize;
2042 npages = size >> LG_PAGE12;
2043
2044 /*
2045 * Mark the extended run as dirty if either portion of the run
2046 * was dirty before allocation. This is rather pedantic,
2047 * because there's not actually any sequence of events that
2048 * could cause the resulting run to be passed to
2049 * arena_run_dalloc() with the dirty argument set to false
2050 * (which is when dirty flag consistency would really matter).
2051 */
2052 flag_dirty = arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind) |
2053 arena_mapbits_dirty_getje_arena_mapbits_dirty_get(chunk, pageind+npages-1);
2054 arena_mapbits_large_setje_arena_mapbits_large_set(chunk, pageind, size, flag_dirty);
2055 arena_mapbits_large_setje_arena_mapbits_large_set(chunk, pageind+npages-1, 0, flag_dirty);
2056
2057 if (config_stats) {
2058 arena->stats.ndalloc_large++;
2059 arena->stats.allocated_large -= oldsize;
2060 arena->stats.lstats[(oldsize >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].ndalloc++;
2061 arena->stats.lstats[(oldsize >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].curruns--;
2062
2063 arena->stats.nmalloc_large++;
2064 arena->stats.nrequests_large++;
2065 arena->stats.allocated_large += size;
2066 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].nmalloc++;
2067 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].nrequests++;
2068 arena->stats.lstats[(size >> LG_PAGE12) - 1].curruns++;
2069 }
2070 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
2071 return (false0);
2072 }
2073 malloc_mutex_unlockje_malloc_mutex_unlock(&arena->lock);
2074
2075 return (true1);
2076}
