2098/*
2099 * Try to resize a large allocation, in order to avoid copying. This will
2100 * always fail if growing an object, and the following run is already in use.
2101 */
2102static bool_Bool
2103arena_ralloc_large(void *ptr, size_t oldsize, size_t size, size_t extra,
2104 bool_Bool zero)
2105{
2106 size_t psize;
2107
2108 psize = PAGE_CEILING(size + extra)(((size + extra) + ((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1))
) & ~((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1)));
2109 if (psize == oldsize) {
2110 /* Same size class. */
2111 return (false0);
2112 } else {
2113 arena_chunk_t *chunk;
2114 arena_t *arena;
2115
2116 chunk = (arena_chunk_t *)CHUNK_ADDR2BASE(ptr)((void *)((uintptr_t)(ptr) & ~je_chunksize_mask));
2117 arena = chunk->arena;
2118
2119 if (psize < oldsize) {
2120 /* Fill before shrinking in order avoid a race. */
2121 arena_ralloc_junk_largeje_arena_ralloc_junk_large(ptr, oldsize, psize);
2122 arena_ralloc_large_shrink(arena, chunk, ptr, oldsize,
2123 psize);
2124 return (false0);
2125 } else {
2126 bool_Bool ret = arena_ralloc_large_grow(arena, chunk, ptr,
2127 oldsize, PAGE_CEILING(size)(((size) + ((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1))) & ~
((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1))),
2128 psize - PAGE_CEILING(size)(((size) + ((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1))) & ~
((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1))), zero);
2129 if (config_fill && ret == false0 && zero == false0) {
2130 if (opt_junkje_opt_junk) {
2131 memset((void *)((uintptr_t)ptr +
2132 oldsize), 0xa5, isallocje_isalloc(ptr,
2133 config_prof) - oldsize);
2134 } else if (opt_zeroje_opt_zero) {
2135 memset((void *)((uintptr_t)ptr +
2136 oldsize), 0, isallocje_isalloc(ptr,
2137 config_prof) - oldsize);
2138 }
2139 }
2140 return (ret);
2141 }
2142 }
2143}
2144
2145bool_Bool
2146arena_ralloc_no_moveje_arena_ralloc_no_move(void *ptr, size_t oldsize, size_t size, size_t extra,
2147 bool_Bool zero)
2148{
2149
2150 /*
2151 * Avoid moving the allocation if the size class can be left the same.
2152 */
2153 if (oldsize <= arena_maxclassje_arena_maxclass) {
2154 if (oldsize <= SMALL_MAXCLASS3584) {
2155 assert(arena_bin_info[SMALL_SIZE2BIN(oldsize)].reg_sizedo { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_bin_info[(je_small_size2bin
[(oldsize-1) >> 3])].reg_size == oldsize)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 2156, "arena_bin_info[SMALL_SIZE2BIN(oldsize)].reg_size == oldsize"
); abort(); } } while (0)
2156 == oldsize)do { if (config_debug && !(je_arena_bin_info[(je_small_size2bin
[(oldsize-1) >> 3])].reg_size == oldsize)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 2156, "arena_bin_info[SMALL_SIZE2BIN(oldsize)].reg_size == oldsize"
); abort(); } } while (0);
2157 if ((size + extra <= SMALL_MAXCLASS3584 &&
2158 SMALL_SIZE2BIN(size + extra)(je_small_size2bin[(size + extra-1) >> 3]) ==
2159 SMALL_SIZE2BIN(oldsize)(je_small_size2bin[(oldsize-1) >> 3])) || (size <= oldsize &&
2160 size + extra >= oldsize))
2161 return (false0);
2162 } else {
2163 assert(size <= arena_maxclass)do { if (config_debug && !(size <= je_arena_maxclass
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 2163, "size <= arena_maxclass"); abort();
} } while (0);
2164 if (size + extra > SMALL_MAXCLASS3584) {
2165 if (arena_ralloc_large(ptr, oldsize, size,
2166 extra, zero) == false0)
2167 return (false0);
2168 }
2169 }
2170 }
2171
2172 /* Reallocation would require a move. */
2173 return (true1);
2174}
2175
2176void *
2177arena_rallocje_arena_ralloc(arena_t *arena, void *ptr, size_t oldsize, size_t size,
2178 size_t extra, size_t alignment, bool_Bool zero, bool_Bool try_tcache_alloc,
2179 bool_Bool try_tcache_dalloc)
2180{
2181 void *ret;
2182 size_t copysize;
2183
2184 /* Try to avoid moving the allocation. */
2185 if (arena_ralloc_no_moveje_arena_ralloc_no_move(ptr, oldsize, size, extra, zero) == false0)
2186 return (ptr);
2187
2188 /*
2189 * size and oldsize are different enough that we need to move the
2190 * object. In that case, fall back to allocating new space and
2191 * copying.
2192 */
2193 if (alignment != 0) {
2194 size_t usize = sa2uje_sa2u(size + extra, alignment);
2195 if (usize == 0)
2196 return (NULL((void*)0));
2197 ret = ipalloctje_ipalloct(usize, alignment, zero, try_tcache_alloc, arena);
2198 } else
2199 ret = arena_mallocje_arena_malloc(arena, size + extra, zero, try_tcache_alloc);
2200
2201 if (ret == NULL((void*)0)) {
2202 if (extra == 0)
2203 return (NULL((void*)0));
2204 /* Try again, this time without extra. */
2205 if (alignment != 0) {
2206 size_t usize = sa2uje_sa2u(size, alignment);
2207 if (usize == 0)
2208 return (NULL((void*)0));
2209 ret = ipalloctje_ipalloct(usize, alignment, zero, try_tcache_alloc,
2210 arena);
2211 } else
2212 ret = arena_mallocje_arena_malloc(arena, size, zero, try_tcache_alloc);
2213
2214 if (ret == NULL((void*)0))
2215 return (NULL((void*)0));
2216 }
2217
2218 /* Junk/zero-filling were already done by ipalloc()/arena_malloc(). */
2219
2220 /*
2221 * Copy at most size bytes (not size+extra), since the caller has no
2222 * expectation that the extra bytes will be reliably preserved.
2223 */
2224 copysize = (size < oldsize) ? size : oldsize;
2225 VALGRIND_MAKE_MEM_UNDEFINED(ret, copysize)do {} while (0);
2226 memcpy(ret, ptr, copysize);
2227 iqalloctje_iqalloct(ptr, try_tcache_dalloc);
2228 return (ret);
2229}

2353/*
2354 * Calculate bin_info->run_size such that it meets the following constraints:
2355 *
2356 * *) bin_info->run_size >= min_run_size
2357 * *) bin_info->run_size <= arena_maxclass
2358 * *) run header overhead <= RUN_MAX_OVRHD (or header overhead relaxed).
2359 * *) bin_info->nregs <= RUN_MAXREGS
2360 *
2361 * bin_info->nregs, bin_info->bitmap_offset, and bin_info->reg0_offset are also
2362 * calculated here, since these settings are all interdependent.
2363 */
2364static size_t
2365bin_info_run_size_calc(arena_bin_info_t *bin_info, size_t min_run_size)
2366{
2367 size_t pad_size;
2368 size_t try_run_size, good_run_size;
2369 uint32_t try_nregs, good_nregs;
2370 uint32_t try_hdr_size, good_hdr_size;
2371 uint32_t try_bitmap_offset, good_bitmap_offset;
2372 uint32_t try_ctx0_offset, good_ctx0_offset;
2373 uint32_t try_redzone0_offset, good_redzone0_offset;
2374
2375 assert(min_run_size >= PAGE)do { if (config_debug && !(min_run_size >= ((size_t
)(1U << 12)))) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 2375, "min_run_size >= PAGE"); abort(); }
} while (0);
2376 assert(min_run_size <= arena_maxclass)do { if (config_debug && !(min_run_size <= je_arena_maxclass
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 2376, "min_run_size <= arena_maxclass"); abort
(); } } while (0);
2377
2378 /*
2379 * Determine redzone size based on minimum alignment and minimum
2380 * redzone size. Add padding to the end of the run if it is needed to
2381 * align the regions. The padding allows each redzone to be half the
2382 * minimum alignment; without the padding, each redzone would have to
2383 * be twice as large in order to maintain alignment.
2384 */
2385 if (config_fill && opt_redzoneje_opt_redzone) {
2386 size_t align_min = ZU(1)((size_t)1) << (ffs(bin_info->reg_size) - 1);
2387 if (align_min <= REDZONE_MINSIZE16) {
2388 bin_info->redzone_size = REDZONE_MINSIZE16;
2389 pad_size = 0;
2390 } else {
2391 bin_info->redzone_size = align_min >> 1;
2392 pad_size = bin_info->redzone_size;
2393 }
2394 } else {
2395 bin_info->redzone_size = 0;
2396 pad_size = 0;
2397 }
2398 bin_info->reg_interval = bin_info->reg_size +
2399 (bin_info->redzone_size << 1);
2400
2401 /*
2402 * Calculate known-valid settings before entering the run_size
2403 * expansion loop, so that the first part of the loop always copies
2404 * valid settings.
2405 *
2406 * The do..while loop iteratively reduces the number of regions until
2407 * the run header and the regions no longer overlap. A closed formula
2408 * would be quite messy, since there is an interdependency between the
2409 * header's mask length and the number of regions.
2410 */
2411 try_run_size = min_run_size;
2412 try_nregs = ((try_run_size - sizeof(arena_run_t)) /
2413 bin_info->reg_interval)
2414 + 1; /* Counter-act try_nregs-- in loop. */
2415 if (try_nregs > RUN_MAXREGS(1U << 11)) {
2416 try_nregs = RUN_MAXREGS(1U << 11)
2417 + 1; /* Counter-act try_nregs-- in loop. */
2418 }
2419 do {
2420 try_nregs--;
2421 try_hdr_size = sizeof(arena_run_t);
2422 /* Pad to a long boundary. */
2423 try_hdr_size = LONG_CEILING(try_hdr_size)(((try_hdr_size) + (((size_t)(1U << 3)) - 1)) & ~((
(size_t)(1U << 3)) - 1));
2424 try_bitmap_offset = try_hdr_size;
2425 /* Add space for bitmap. */
2426 try_hdr_size += bitmap_sizeje_bitmap_size(try_nregs);
2427 if (config_prof && opt_profje_opt_prof && prof_promoteje_prof_promote == false0) {
2428 /* Pad to a quantum boundary. */
2429 try_hdr_size = QUANTUM_CEILING(try_hdr_size)(((try_hdr_size) + (((size_t)(1U << 4)) - 1)) & ~((
(size_t)(1U << 4)) - 1));
2430 try_ctx0_offset = try_hdr_size;
2431 /* Add space for one (prof_ctx_t *) per region. */
2432 try_hdr_size += try_nregs * sizeof(prof_ctx_t *);
2433 } else
2434 try_ctx0_offset = 0;
2435 try_redzone0_offset = try_run_size - (try_nregs *
2436 bin_info->reg_interval) - pad_size;
2437 } while (try_hdr_size > try_redzone0_offset);
2438
2439 /* run_size expansion loop. */
2440 do {
2441 /*
2442 * Copy valid settings before trying more aggressive settings.
2443 */
2444 good_run_size = try_run_size;
2445 good_nregs = try_nregs;
2446 good_hdr_size = try_hdr_size;
2447 good_bitmap_offset = try_bitmap_offset;
2448 good_ctx0_offset = try_ctx0_offset;
2449 good_redzone0_offset = try_redzone0_offset;
2450
2451 /* Try more aggressive settings. */
2452 try_run_size += PAGE((size_t)(1U << 12));
2453 try_nregs = ((try_run_size - sizeof(arena_run_t) - pad_size) /
2454 bin_info->reg_interval)
2455 + 1; /* Counter-act try_nregs-- in loop. */
2456 if (try_nregs > RUN_MAXREGS(1U << 11)) {
2457 try_nregs = RUN_MAXREGS(1U << 11)
2458 + 1; /* Counter-act try_nregs-- in loop. */
2459 }
2460 do {
2461 try_nregs--;
2462 try_hdr_size = sizeof(arena_run_t);
2463 /* Pad to a long boundary. */
2464 try_hdr_size = LONG_CEILING(try_hdr_size)(((try_hdr_size) + (((size_t)(1U << 3)) - 1)) & ~((
(size_t)(1U << 3)) - 1));

2466 /* Add space for bitmap. */
2467 try_hdr_size += bitmap_sizeje_bitmap_size(try_nregs);
2468 if (config_prof && opt_profje_opt_prof && prof_promoteje_prof_promote == false0) {
2469 /* Pad to a quantum boundary. */
2470 try_hdr_size = QUANTUM_CEILING(try_hdr_size)(((try_hdr_size) + (((size_t)(1U << 4)) - 1)) & ~((
(size_t)(1U << 4)) - 1));
2471 try_ctx0_offset = try_hdr_size;
2472 /*
2473 * Add space for one (prof_ctx_t *) per region.
2474 */
2475 try_hdr_size += try_nregs *
2476 sizeof(prof_ctx_t *);
2477 }
2478 try_redzone0_offset = try_run_size - (try_nregs *
2479 bin_info->reg_interval) - pad_size;
2480 } while (try_hdr_size > try_redzone0_offset);
2481 } while (try_run_size <= arena_maxclassje_arena_maxclass
2482 && RUN_MAX_OVRHD0x0000003dU * (bin_info->reg_interval << 3) >
2483 RUN_MAX_OVRHD_RELAX0x00001800U
2484 && (try_redzone0_offset << RUN_BFP12) > RUN_MAX_OVRHD0x0000003dU * try_run_size
2485 && try_nregs < RUN_MAXREGS(1U << 11));
2486
2487 assert(good_hdr_size <= good_redzone0_offset)do { if (config_debug && !(good_hdr_size <= good_redzone0_offset
)) { je_malloc_printf( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n"
, "src/arena.c", 2487, "good_hdr_size <= good_redzone0_offset"
); abort(); } } while (0);
2488
2489 /* Copy final settings. */
2490 bin_info->run_size = good_run_size;
2491 bin_info->nregs = good_nregs;
2492 bin_info->bitmap_offset = good_bitmap_offset;
2493 bin_info->ctx0_offset = good_ctx0_offset;
2494 bin_info->reg0_offset = good_redzone0_offset + bin_info->redzone_size;
2495
2496 assert(bin_info->reg0_offset - bin_info->redzone_size + (bin_info->nregsdo { if (config_debug && !(bin_info->reg0_offset -
bin_info->redzone_size + (bin_info->nregs * bin_info->
reg_interval) + pad_size == bin_info->run_size)) { je_malloc_printf

, 2497, "bin_info->reg0_offset - bin_info->redzone_size + (bin_info->nregs * bin_info->reg_interval) + pad_size == bin_info->run_size"
); abort(); } } while (0)
2497 * bin_info->reg_interval) + pad_size == bin_info->run_size)do { if (config_debug && !(bin_info->reg0_offset -
bin_info->redzone_size + (bin_info->nregs * bin_info->
reg_interval) + pad_size == bin_info->run_size)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 2497, "bin_info->reg0_offset - bin_info->redzone_size + (bin_info->nregs * bin_info->reg_interval) + pad_size == bin_info->run_size"
); abort(); } } while (0);
2498
2499 return (good_run_size);
2500}

2516
2517void
2518arena_bootje_arena_boot(void)
2519{
2520 size_t header_size;
2521 unsigned i;
2522
2523 /*
2524 * Compute the header size such that it is large enough to contain the
2525 * page map. The page map is biased to omit entries for the header
2526 * itself, so some iteration is necessary to compute the map bias.
2527 *
2528 * 1) Compute safe header_size and map_bias values that include enough
2529 * space for an unbiased page map.
2530 * 2) Refine map_bias based on (1) to omit the header pages in the page
2531 * map. The resulting map_bias may be one too small.
2532 * 3) Refine map_bias based on (2). The result will be >= the result
2533 * from (2), and will always be correct.
2534 */
2535 map_biasje_map_bias = 0;
2536 for (i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
2537 header_size = offsetof(arena_chunk_t, map)__builtin_offsetof(arena_chunk_t, map) +
2538 (sizeof(arena_chunk_map_t) * (chunk_npagesje_chunk_npages-map_biasje_map_bias));
2539 map_biasje_map_bias = (header_size >> LG_PAGE12) + ((header_size & PAGE_MASK((size_t)(((size_t)(1U << 12)) - 1)))
2540 != 0);
2541 }
2542 assert(map_bias > 0)do { if (config_debug && !(je_map_bias > 0)) { je_malloc_printf
( "<jemalloc>: %s:%d: Failed assertion: \"%s\"\n", "src/arena.c"
, 2542, "map_bias > 0"); abort(); } } while (0);
2543
2544 arena_maxclassje_arena_maxclass = chunksizeje_chunksize - (map_biasje_map_bias << LG_PAGE12);
2545
2546 bin_info_init();
2547}
